 $filters.removeClass('selected');$this.addClass('selected');$isotope.isotope({filter:'.'+$this.attr('data-option-value')})});if(default_section!==''){$('#cs-226547360 .box-heading a[data-option-value="section-'+default_section+'"]').click();}
